<pr_description>
1.42.0 breaks existing justfiles around modules with imports
Given the following justfiles, `just a::foo` and `just b::foo` both print `A`, when `just b::foo` should print `B`.

```just
# justfile
mod a
mod b
```

```just
# a.just
X := 'A'
import 'shared.just'
```

```just
# b.just
X := 'B'
import 'shared.just'
```

```just
# shared.just
foo:
  @echo {{ X }}
```

</pr_description>

     1	use {super::*, TokenKind::*};

     3	/// Just language parser
     4	///
     5	/// The parser is a (hopefully) straightforward recursive descent parser.
     6	///
     7	/// It uses a few tokens of lookahead to disambiguate different constructs.
     8	///
     9	/// The `expect_*` and `presume_`* methods are similar in that they assert the
    10	/// type of unparsed tokens and consume them. However, upon encountering an
    11	/// unexpected token, the `expect_*` methods return an unexpected token error,
    12	/// whereas the `presume_*` tokens return an internal error.
    13	///
    14	/// The `presume_*` methods are used when the token stream has been inspected in
    15	/// some other way, and thus encountering an unexpected token is a bug in Just,
    16	/// and not a syntax error.
    17	///
    18	/// All methods starting with `parse_*` parse and return a language construct.
    19	///
    20	/// The parser tracks an expected set of tokens as it parses. This set contains
    21	/// all tokens which would have been accepted at the current point in the
    22	/// parse. Whenever the parser tests for a token that would be accepted, but
    23	/// does not find it, it adds that token to the set. When the parser accepts a
    24	/// token, the set is cleared. If the parser finds a token which is unexpected,
    25	/// the elements of the set are printed in the resultant error message.
    26	pub(crate) struct Parser<'run, 'src> {
    27	  expected_tokens: BTreeSet<TokenKind>,
    28	  file_depth: u32,
    29	  import_offsets: Vec<usize>,
    30	  module_namepath: Option<&'run Namepath<'src>>,
    31	  next_token: usize,
    32	  recursion_depth: usize,
    33	  tokens: &'run [Token<'src>],
    34	  unstable_features: BTreeSet<UnstableFeature>,
    35	  working_directory: &'run Path,
    36	}
    37	
    38	impl<'run, 'src> Parser<'run, 'src> {

    40	  pub(crate) fn parse(

    44	    tokens: &'run [Token<'src>],
    45	    working_directory: &'run Path,
    46	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Ast<'src>> {
    47	    Self {

    62	    Ok(self.next()?.error(kind))

    65	  /// Construct an unexpected token error with the token returned by

    67	  fn unexpected_token(&self) -> CompileResult<'src, CompileError<'src>> {
    68	    self.error(CompileErrorKind::UnexpectedToken {
    69	      expected: self
    70	        .expected_tokens
    71	        .iter()
    72	        .copied()
    73	        .filter(|kind| *kind != ByteOrderMark)
    74	        .collect::<Vec<TokenKind>>(),
    75	      found: self.next()?.kind,
    76	    })
    77	  }

    79	  fn internal_error(&self, message: impl Into<String>) -> CompileResult<'src, CompileError<'src>> {
    80	    self.error(CompileErrorKind::Internal {
    81	      message: message.into(),
    82	    })
    83	  }

    85	  /// An iterator over the remaining significant tokens
    86	  fn rest(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = Token<'src>> + 'run {
    87	    self.tokens[self.next_token..]
    88	      .iter()
    89	      .copied()
    90	      .filter(|token| token.kind != Whitespace)
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  /// The next significant token
    94	  fn next(&self) -> CompileResult<'src, Token<'src>> {
    95	    if let Some(token) = self.rest().next() {
    96	      Ok(token)
    97	    } else {
    98	      Err(self.internal_error("`Parser::next()` called after end of token stream")?)
    99	    }
   100	  }
   101	
   102	  /// Check if the next significant token is of kind `kind`
   103	  fn next_is(&mut self, kind: TokenKind) -> bool {
   104	    self.next_are(&[kind])
   105	  }
   106	
   107	  /// Check if the next significant tokens are of kinds `kinds`
   108	  ///
   109	  /// The first token in `kinds` will be added to the expected token set.
   110	  fn next_are(&mut self, kinds: &[TokenKind]) -> bool {
   111	    if let Some(&kind) = kinds.first() {
   112	      self.expected_tokens.insert(kind);
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    let mut rest = self.rest();
   116	    for kind in kinds {
   117	      match rest.next() {
   118	        Some(token) => {
   119	          if token.kind != *kind {
   120	            return false;
   121	          }
   122	        }
   123	        None => return false,
   124	      }
   125	    }
   126	    true
   127	  }
   128	
   129	  /// Advance past one significant token, clearing the expected token set.
   130	  fn advance(&mut self) -> CompileResult<'src, Token<'src>> {
   131	    self.expected_tokens.clear();
   132	
   133	    for skipped in &self.tokens[self.next_token..] {
   134	      self.next_token += 1;
   135	
   136	      if skipped.kind != Whitespace {
   137	        return Ok(*skipped);
   138	      }
   139	    }

   141	    Err(self.internal_error("`Parser::advance()` advanced past end of token stream")?)
   142	  }

   144	  /// Return the next token if it is of kind `expected`, otherwise, return an
   145	  /// unexpected token error
   146	  fn expect(&mut self, expected: TokenKind) -> CompileResult<'src, Token<'src>> {
   147	    if let Some(token) = self.accept(expected)? {
   148	      Ok(token)
   149	    } else {
   150	      Err(self.unexpected_token()?)

   154	  /// Return an unexpected token error if the next token is not an EOL
   155	  fn expect_eol(&mut self) -> CompileResult<'src> {
   156	    self.accept(Comment)?;
   157	
   158	    if self.next_is(Eof) {
   159	      return Ok(());
   160	    }
   161	
   162	    self.expect(Eol).map(|_| ())
   163	  }

   165	  fn expect_keyword(&mut self, expected: Keyword) -> CompileResult<'src> {
   166	    let found = self.advance()?;
   167	
   168	    if found.kind == Identifier && expected == found.lexeme() {
   169	      Ok(())
   170	    } else {
   171	      Err(found.error(CompileErrorKind::ExpectedKeyword {
   172	        expected: vec![expected],
   173	        found,
   174	      }))
   175	    }
   176	  }

   178	  /// Return an internal error if the next token is not of kind `Identifier`
   179	  /// with lexeme `lexeme`.
   180	  fn presume_keyword(&mut self, keyword: Keyword) -> CompileResult<'src> {
   181	    let next = self.advance()?;
   182	
   183	    if next.kind != Identifier {
   184	      Err(self.internal_error(format!(
   185	        "Presumed next token would have kind {Identifier}, but found {}",
   186	        next.kind

   188	    } else if keyword == next.lexeme() {
   189	      Ok(())
   190	    } else {

   192	        "Presumed next token would have lexeme \"{keyword}\", but found \"{}\"",
   193	        next.lexeme(),

   195	    }
   196	  }
   197	
   198	  /// Return an internal error if the next token is not of kind `kind`.
   199	  fn presume(&mut self, kind: TokenKind) -> CompileResult<'src, Token<'src>> {
   200	    let next = self.advance()?;
   201	
   202	    if next.kind == kind {
   203	      Ok(next)
   204	    } else {
   205	      Err(self.internal_error(format!(
   206	        "Presumed next token would have kind {kind:?}, but found {:?}",
   207	        next.kind
   208	      ))?)
   209	    }
   210	  }
   211	
   212	  /// Return an internal error if the next token is not one of kinds `kinds`.
   213	  fn presume_any(&mut self, kinds: &[TokenKind]) -> CompileResult<'src, Token<'src>> {
   214	    let next = self.advance()?;
   215	    if kinds.contains(&next.kind) {
   216	      Ok(next)
   217	    } else {
   218	      Err(self.internal_error(format!(
   219	        "Presumed next token would be {}, but found {}",
   220	        List::or(kinds),
   221	        next.kind
   222	      ))?)
   223	    }
   224	  }
   225	
   226	  /// Accept and return a token of kind `kind`
   227	  fn accept(&mut self, kind: TokenKind) -> CompileResult<'src, Option<Token<'src>>> {
   228	    if self.next_is(kind) {
   229	      Ok(Some(self.advance()?))
   230	    } else {
   231	      Ok(None)
   232	    }
   233	  }
   234	
   235	  /// Return an error if the next token is of kind `forbidden`
   236	  fn forbid<F>(&self, forbidden: TokenKind, error: F) -> CompileResult<'src>
   237	  where
   238	    F: FnOnce(Token) -> CompileError,
   239	  {
   240	    let next = self.next()?;
   241	
   242	    if next.kind == forbidden {
   243	      Err(error(next))
   244	    } else {
   245	      Ok(())
   246	    }
   247	  }
   248	
   249	  /// Accept a double-colon separated sequence of identifiers
   250	  fn accept_namepath(&mut self) -> CompileResult<'src, Option<Namepath<'src>>> {
   251	    if self.next_is(Identifier) {
   252	      Ok(Some(self.parse_namepath()?))
   253	    } else {
   254	      Ok(None)
   255	    }
   256	  }
   257	
   258	  fn accepted_keyword(&mut self, keyword: Keyword) -> CompileResult<'src, bool> {
   259	    let next = self.next()?;
   260	
   261	    if next.kind == Identifier && next.lexeme() == keyword.lexeme() {
   262	      self.advance()?;
   263	      Ok(true)
   264	    } else {
   265	      Ok(false)
   266	    }
   267	  }
   268	
   269	  /// Accept a dependency
   270	  fn accept_dependency(&mut self) -> CompileResult<'src, Option<UnresolvedDependency<'src>>> {
   271	    if let Some(recipe) = self.accept_namepath()? {
   272	      Ok(Some(UnresolvedDependency {
   273	        arguments: Vec::new(),
   274	        recipe,
   275	      }))
   276	    } else if self.accepted(ParenL)? {
   277	      let recipe = self.parse_namepath()?;
   278	
   279	      let mut arguments = Vec::new();
   280	
   281	      while !self.accepted(ParenR)? {
   282	        arguments.push(self.parse_expression()?);
   283	      }
   284	
   285	      Ok(Some(UnresolvedDependency { arguments, recipe }))
   286	    } else {
   287	      Ok(None)
   288	    }
   289	  }
   290	
   291	  /// Accept and return `true` if next token is of kind `kind`
   292	  fn accepted(&mut self, kind: TokenKind) -> CompileResult<'src, bool> {
   293	    Ok(self.accept(kind)?.is_some())
   294	  }

   296	  /// Parse a justfile, consumes self
   297	  fn parse_ast(mut self) -> CompileResult<'src, Ast<'src>> {
   298	    fn pop_doc_comment<'src>(
   299	      items: &mut Vec<Item<'src>>,
   300	      eol_since_last_comment: bool,
   301	    ) -> Option<&'src str> {
   302	      if !eol_since_last_comment {
   303	        if let Some(Item::Comment(contents)) = items.last() {
   304	          let doc = Some(contents[1..].trim_start());
   305	          items.pop();
   306	          return doc;
   307	        }
   308	      }
   309	
   310	      None
   311	    }
   312	
   313	    let mut items = Vec::new();
   314	
   315	    let mut eol_since_last_comment = false;
   316	
   317	    self.accept(ByteOrderMark)?;
   318	
   319	    loop {
   320	      let mut attributes = self.parse_attributes()?;
   321	      let mut take_attributes = || {
   322	        attributes
   323	          .take()
   324	          .map(|(_token, attributes)| attributes)
   325	          .unwrap_or_default()
   326	      };
   327	
   328	      let next = self.next()?;
   329	
   330	      if let Some(comment) = self.accept(Comment)? {
   331	        items.push(Item::Comment(comment.lexeme().trim_end()));
   332	        self.expect_eol()?;
   333	        eol_since_last_comment = false;
   334	      } else if self.accepted(Eol)? {
   335	        eol_since_last_comment = true;
   336	      } else if self.accepted(Eof)? {
   337	        break;
   338	      } else if self.next_is(Identifier) {
   339	        match Keyword::from_lexeme(next.lexeme()) {
   340	          Some(Keyword::Alias) if self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, ColonEquals]) => {
   341	            items.push(Item::Alias(self.parse_alias(take_attributes())?));
   342	          }
   343	          Some(Keyword::Export) if self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, ColonEquals]) => {
   344	            self.presume_keyword(Keyword::Export)?;
   345	            items.push(Item::Assignment(
   346	              self.parse_assignment(true, take_attributes())?,
   347	            ));
   348	          }
   349	          Some(Keyword::Unexport)
   350	            if self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Eof])
   351	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Eol]) =>
   352	          {
   353	            self.presume_keyword(Keyword::Unexport)?;
   354	            let name = self.parse_name()?;
   355	            self.expect_eol()?;
   356	            items.push(Item::Unexport { name });
   357	          }
   358	          Some(Keyword::Import)
   359	            if self.next_are(&[Identifier, StringToken])
   360	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, StringToken])
   361	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, QuestionMark]) =>
   362	          {
   363	            self.presume_keyword(Keyword::Import)?;
   364	            let optional = self.accepted(QuestionMark)?;
   365	            let (path, relative) = self.parse_string_literal_token()?;
   366	            items.push(Item::Import {
   367	              absolute: None,
   368	              optional,
   369	              path,
   370	              relative,
   371	            });
   372	          }
   373	          Some(Keyword::Mod)
   374	            if self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Comment])
   375	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Eof])
   376	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Eol])
   377	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Identifier, StringToken])
   378	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, StringToken])
   379	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, QuestionMark]) =>
   380	          {
   381	            let doc = pop_doc_comment(&mut items, eol_since_last_comment);
   382	
   383	            self.presume_keyword(Keyword::Mod)?;
   384	
   385	            let optional = self.accepted(QuestionMark)?;
   386	
   387	            let name = self.parse_name()?;
   388	
   389	            let relative = if self.next_is(StringToken) || self.next_are(&[Identifier, StringToken])
   390	            {
   391	              Some(self.parse_string_literal()?)
   392	            } else {
   393	              None
   394	            };
   395	
   396	            let attributes = take_attributes();
   397	
   398	            attributes.ensure_valid_attributes(
   399	              "Module",
   400	              *name,
   401	              &[AttributeDiscriminant::Doc, AttributeDiscriminant::Group],
   402	            )?;
   403	
   404	            let doc = match attributes.get(AttributeDiscriminant::Doc) {
   405	              Some(Attribute::Doc(Some(doc))) => Some(doc.cooked.clone()),
   406	              Some(Attribute::Doc(None)) => None,
   407	              None => doc.map(ToOwned::to_owned),
   408	              _ => unreachable!(),
   409	            };
   410	
   411	            let mut groups = Vec::new();
   412	            for attribute in attributes {
   413	              if let Attribute::Group(group) = attribute {
   414	                groups.push(group.cooked);
   415	              }
   416	            }
   417	
   418	            items.push(Item::Module {
   419	              groups,
   420	              absolute: None,
   421	              doc,
   422	              name,
   423	              optional,
   424	              relative,
   425	            });
   426	          }
   427	          Some(Keyword::Set)
   428	            if self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, ColonEquals])
   429	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Comment, Eof])
   430	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Comment, Eol])
   431	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Eof])
   432	              || self.next_are(&[Identifier, Identifier, Eol]) =>
   433	          {
   434	            items.push(Item::Set(self.parse_set()?));
   435	          }
   436	          _ => {
   437	            if self.next_are(&[Identifier, ColonEquals]) {
   438	              items.push(Item::Assignment(
   439	                self.parse_assignment(false, take_attributes())?,
   440	              ));
   441	            } else {
   442	              let doc = pop_doc_comment(&mut items, eol_since_last_comment);
   443	              items.push(Item::Recipe(self.parse_recipe(
   444	                take_attributes(),
   445	                doc,
   446	                false,
   447	              )?));
   448	            }
   449	          }
   450	        }
   451	      } else if self.accepted(At)? {
   452	        let doc = pop_doc_comment(&mut items, eol_since_last_comment);
   453	        items.push(Item::Recipe(self.parse_recipe(
   454	          take_attributes(),
   455	          doc,
   456	          true,
   457	        )?));
   458	      } else {
   459	        return Err(self.unexpected_token()?);
   460	      }
   461	
   462	      if let Some((token, attributes)) = attributes {
   463	        return Err(token.error(CompileErrorKind::ExtraneousAttributes {
   464	          count: attributes.len(),
   465	        }));
   466	      }
   467	    }
   468	
   469	    if self.next_token != self.tokens.len() {
   470	      return Err(self.internal_error(format!(
   471	        "Parse completed with {} unparsed tokens",
   472	        self.tokens.len() - self.next_token,
   473	      ))?);
   474	    }
   475	
   476	    Ok(Ast {
   477	      items,
   478	      module_path: self
   479	        .module_namepath
   480	        .map(ToString::to_string)
   481	        .unwrap_or_default(),
   482	      unstable_features: self.unstable_features,
   483	      warnings: Vec::new(),
   484	      working_directory: self.working_directory.into(),
   485	    })
   486	  }

   488	  /// Parse an alias, e.g `alias name := target`
   489	  fn parse_alias(
   490	    &mut self,
   491	    attributes: AttributeSet<'src>,
   492	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Alias<'src, Namepath<'src>>> {
   493	    self.presume_keyword(Keyword::Alias)?;
   494	    let name = self.parse_name()?;
   495	    self.presume_any(&[Equals, ColonEquals])?;
   496	    let target = self.parse_namepath()?;
   497	    self.expect_eol()?;
   498

   500	
   501	    Ok(Alias {
   502	      attributes,
   503	      name,
   504	      target,
   505	    })
   506	  }

    16	    asts: &'run HashMap<PathBuf, Ast<'src>>,

    18	    groups: &[String],

    27	  fn justfile(
    28	    mut self,
    29	    asts: &'run HashMap<PathBuf, Ast<'src>>,
    30	    doc: Option<String>,
    31	    groups: &[String],
    32	    loaded: &[PathBuf],
    33	    name: Option<Name<'src>>,
    34	    paths: &HashMap<PathBuf, PathBuf>,
    35	    root: &Path,
    36	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Justfile<'src>> {
    37	    let mut definitions = HashMap::new();
    38	    let mut imports = HashSet::new();
    39	    let mut unstable_features = BTreeSet::new();
    40	
    41	    let mut stack = Vec::new();
    42	    let ast = asts.get(root).unwrap();
    43	    stack.push(ast);
    44	
    45	    while let Some(ast) = stack.pop() {
    46	      unstable_features.extend(&ast.unstable_features);
    47	
    48	      for item in &ast.items {
    49	        match item {
    50	          Item::Alias(alias) => {
    51	            Self::define(&mut definitions, alias.name, "alias", false)?;
    52	            self.aliases.insert(alias.clone());
    53	          }
    54	          Item::Assignment(assignment) => {
    55	            self.assignments.push(assignment);
    56	          }
    57	          Item::Comment(_) => (),
    58	          Item::Import { absolute, .. } => {
    59	            if let Some(absolute) = absolute {
    60	              if imports.insert(absolute) {
    61	                stack.push(asts.get(absolute).unwrap());
    62	              }
    63	            }
    64	          }
    65	          Item::Module {
    66	            absolute,
    67	            doc,
    68	            groups,
    69	            name,
    70	            ..
    71	          } => {
    72	            if let Some(absolute) = absolute {
    73	              Self::define(&mut definitions, *name, "module", false)?;
    74	              self.modules.insert(Self::analyze(
    75	                asts,
    76	                doc.clone(),
    77	                groups.as_slice(),
    78	                loaded,
    79	                Some(*name),
    80	                paths,
    81	                absolute,
    82	              )?);
    83	            }
    84	          }
    85	          Item::Recipe(recipe) => {
    86	            if recipe.enabled() {
    87	              Self::analyze_recipe(recipe)?;
    88	              self.recipes.push(recipe);
    89	            }
    90	          }
    91	          Item::Set(set) => {
    92	            self.analyze_set(set)?;
    93	            self.sets.insert(set.clone());
    94	          }
    95	          Item::Unexport { name } => {
    96	            if !self.unexports.insert(name.lexeme().to_string()) {
    97	              return Err(name.token.error(DuplicateUnexport {
    98	                variable: name.lexeme(),
    99	              }));
   100	            }
   101	          }
   102	        }
   103	      }
   104	
   105	      self.warnings.extend(ast.warnings.iter().cloned());
   106	    }
   107	
   108	    let settings = Settings::from_table(self.sets);
   109	
   110	    let mut assignments: Table<'src, Assignment<'src>> = Table::default();
   111	    for assignment in self.assignments {
   112	      let variable = assignment.name.lexeme();
   113	
   114	      if !settings.allow_duplicate_variables && assignments.contains_key(variable) {
   115	        return Err(assignment.name.token.error(DuplicateVariable { variable }));
   116	      }
   117	
   118	      if assignments.get(variable).map_or(true, |original| {
   119	        assignment.file_depth <= original.file_depth
   120	      }) {
   121	        assignments.insert(assignment.clone());
   122	      }
   123	
   124	      if self.unexports.contains(variable) {
   125	        return Err(assignment.name.token.error(ExportUnexported { variable }));
   126	      }
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    AssignmentResolver::resolve_assignments(&assignments)?;
   130	
   131	    let mut deduplicated_recipes = Table::<'src, UnresolvedRecipe<'src>>::default();
   132	    for recipe in self.recipes {
   133	      Self::define(
   134	        &mut definitions,
   135	        recipe.name,
   136	        "recipe",
   137	        settings.allow_duplicate_recipes,
   138	      )?;
   139

   143	      {
   144	        deduplicated_recipes.insert(recipe.clone());
   145	      }
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    let recipes = RecipeResolver::resolve_recipes(
   149	      &assignments,
   150	      &self.modules,
   151	      &settings,
   152	      deduplicated_recipes,
   153	    )?;
   154

   156	    while let Some(alias) = self.aliases.pop() {
   157	      aliases.insert(Self::resolve_alias(&self.modules, &recipes, alias)?);
   158	    }
   159

   161	      if recipe.attributes.contains(AttributeDiscriminant::Script) {
   162	        unstable_features.insert(UnstableFeature::ScriptAttribute);
   163	        break;
   164	      }
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    if settings.script_interpreter.is_some() {
   168	      unstable_features.insert(UnstableFeature::ScriptInterpreterSetting);
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    let source = root.to_owned();
   172	    let root = paths.get(root).unwrap();
   173

   176	      assignments,
   177	      default: recipes
   178	        .values()

   180	        .fold(None, |accumulator, next| match accumulator {
   181	          None => Some(Arc::clone(next)),
   182	          Some(previous) => Some(if previous.line_number() < next.line_number() {
   183	            previous
   184	          } else {

   186	          }),
   187	        }),

   194	      recipes,
   195	      settings,
   196	      source,
   197	      unexports: self.unexports,
   198	      unstable_features,
   199	      warnings: self.warnings,
   200	      working_directory: ast.working_directory.clone(),
   201	    })
   202	  }

   204	  fn define(
   205	    definitions: &mut HashMap<&'src str, (&'static str, Name<'src>)>,
   206	    name: Name<'src>,
   207	    second_type: &'static str,
   208	    duplicates_allowed: bool,
   209	  ) -> CompileResult<'src> {
   210	    if let Some((first_type, original)) = definitions.get(name.lexeme()) {
   211	      if !(*first_type == second_type && duplicates_allowed) {
   212	        let ((first_type, second_type), (original, redefinition)) = if name.line < original.line {
   213	          ((second_type, *first_type), (name, *original))
   214	        } else {
   215	          ((*first_type, second_type), (*original, name))
   216	        };
   217	
   218	        return Err(redefinition.token.error(Redefinition {
   219	          first_type,
   220	          second_type,
   221	          name: name.lexeme(),
   222	          first: original.line,
   223	        }));
   224	      }
   225	    }
   226	
   227	    definitions.insert(name.lexeme(), (second_type, name));
   228	
   229	    Ok(())
   230	  }
   231	
   232	  fn analyze_recipe(recipe: &UnresolvedRecipe<'src>) -> CompileResult<'src> {
   233	    let mut parameters = BTreeSet::new();
   234	    let mut passed_default = false;
   235	
   236	    for parameter in &recipe.parameters {
   237	      if parameters.contains(parameter.name.lexeme()) {
   238	        return Err(parameter.name.token.error(DuplicateParameter {
   239	          recipe: recipe.name.lexeme(),
   240	          parameter: parameter.name.lexeme(),
   241	        }));
   242	      }
   243	
   244	      parameters.insert(parameter.name.lexeme());
   245	
   246	      if parameter.default.is_some() {
   247	        passed_default = true;
   248	      } else if passed_default && parameter.is_required() {
   249	        return Err(
   250	          parameter
   251	            .name
   252	            .token
   253	            .error(RequiredParameterFollowsDefaultParameter {
   254	              parameter: parameter.name.lexeme(),
   255	            }),
   256	        );
   257	      }
   258	    }
   259	
   260	    let mut continued = false;
   261	    for line in &recipe.body {
   262	      if !recipe.is_script() && !continued {
   263	        if let Some(Fragment::Text { token }) = line.fragments.first() {
   264	          let text = token.lexeme();
   265	
   266	          if text.starts_with(' ') || text.starts_with('\t') {
   267	            return Err(token.error(ExtraLeadingWhitespace));
   268	          }
   269	        }
   270	      }
   271	
   272	      continued = line.is_continuation();
   273	    }
   274	
   275	    if !recipe.is_script() {
   276	      if let Some(attribute) = recipe.attributes.get(AttributeDiscriminant::Extension) {
   277	        return Err(recipe.name.error(InvalidAttribute {
   278	          item_kind: "Recipe",
   279	          item_name: recipe.name.lexeme(),
   280	          attribute: attribute.clone(),
   281	        }));
   282	      }
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    Ok(())
   286	  }
   287	
   288	  fn analyze_set(&self, set: &Set<'src>) -> CompileResult<'src> {
   289	    if let Some(original) = self.sets.get(set.name.lexeme()) {
   290	      return Err(set.name.error(DuplicateSet {
   291	        setting: original.name.lexeme(),
   292	        first: original.name.line,
   293	      }));
   294	    }
   295	
   296	    Ok(())
   297	  }
   298	
   299	  fn resolve_alias<'a>(
   300	    modules: &'a Table<'src, Justfile<'src>>,
   301	    recipes: &'a Table<'src, Arc<Recipe<'src>>>,
   302	    alias: Alias<'src, Namepath<'src>>,
   303	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Alias<'src>> {
   304	    match Self::resolve_recipe(&alias.target, modules, recipes) {
   305	      Some(target) => Ok(alias.resolve(target)),
   306	      None => Err(alias.name.token.error(UnknownAliasTarget {
   307	        alias: alias.name.lexeme(),
   308	        target: alias.target,
   309	      })),
   310	    }
   311	  }
   312	
   313	  pub(crate) fn resolve_recipe<'a>(
   314	    path: &Namepath<'src>,
   315	    mut modules: &'a Table<'src, Justfile<'src>>,
   316	    mut recipes: &'a Table<'src, Arc<Recipe<'src>>>,
   317	  ) -> Option<Arc<Recipe<'src>>> {
   318	    let (name, path) = path.split_last();
   319	
   320	    for name in path {
   321	      let module = modules.get(name.lexeme())?;
   322	      modules = &module.modules;
   323	      recipes = &module.recipes;
   324	    }
   325	
   326	    recipes.get(name.lexeme()).cloned()
   327	  }
   328	}

     2	
     3	pub(crate) struct Loader {
     4	  paths: Arena<PathBuf>,
     5	  srcs: Arena<String>,
     6	}
     7	
     8	impl Loader {
     9	  pub(crate) fn new() -> Self {
    10	    Self {
    11	      srcs: Arena::new(),
    12	      paths: Arena::new(),
    13	    }
    14	  }
    15	
    16	  pub(crate) fn load<'src>(
    17	    &'src self,
    18	    root: &Path,
    19	    path: &Path,
    20	  ) -> RunResult<'src, (&'src Path, &'src str)> {
    21	    let src = fs::read_to_string(path).map_err(|io_error| Error::Load {
    22	      path: path.into(),
    23	      io_error,
    24	    })?;
    25	
    26	    let relative = path.strip_prefix(root.parent().unwrap()).unwrap_or(path);
    27	
    28	    Ok((self.paths.alloc(relative.into()), self.srcs.alloc(src)))
    29	  }
    30	}

     5	impl Compiler {
     6	  pub(crate) fn compile<'src>(
     7	    loader: &'src Loader,
     8	    root: &Path,
     9	  ) -> RunResult<'src, Compilation<'src>> {
    10	    let mut asts = HashMap::<PathBuf, Ast>::new();
    11	    let mut loaded = Vec::new();
    12	    let mut paths = HashMap::<PathBuf, PathBuf>::new();
    13	    let mut srcs = HashMap::<PathBuf, &str>::new();
    14	
    15	    let mut stack = Vec::new();
    16	    stack.push(Source::root(root));
    17	
    18	    while let Some(current) = stack.pop() {
    19	      let (relative, src) = loader.load(root, &current.path)?;
    20	      loaded.push(relative.into());
    21	      let tokens = Lexer::lex(relative, src)?;
    22	      let mut ast = Parser::parse(
    23	        current.file_depth,
    24	        &current.import_offsets,
    25	        current.namepath.as_ref(),
    26	        &tokens,
    27	        &current.working_directory,
    28	      )?;
    29	
    30	      paths.insert(current.path.clone(), relative.into());
    31	      srcs.insert(current.path.clone(), src);
    32	
    33	      for item in &mut ast.items {
    34	        match item {
    35	          Item::Module {
    36	            absolute,
    37	            name,
    38	            optional,
    39	            relative,
    40	            ..
    41	          } => {
    42	            let parent = current.path.parent().unwrap();
    43	
    44	            let relative = relative
    45	              .as_ref()
    46	              .map(|relative| Self::expand_tilde(&relative.cooked))
    47	              .transpose()?;
    48	
    49	            let import = Self::find_module_file(parent, *name, relative.as_deref())?;
    50	
    51	            if let Some(import) = import {
    52	              if current.file_path.contains(&import) {
    53	                return Err(Error::CircularImport {
    54	                  current: current.path,
    55	                  import,
    56	                });
    57	              }
    58	              *absolute = Some(import.clone());
    59	              stack.push(current.module(*name, import));
    60	            } else if !*optional {
    61	              return Err(Error::MissingModuleFile { module: *name });
    62	            }
    63	          }
    64	          Item::Import {
    65	            relative,
    66	            absolute,
    67	            optional,
    68	            path,
    69	          } => {
    70	            let import = current
    71	              .path
    72	              .parent()
    73	              .unwrap()
    74	              .join(Self::expand_tilde(&relative.cooked)?)
    75	              .lexiclean();
    76	
    77	            if import.is_file() {
    78	              if current.file_path.contains(&import) {
    79	                return Err(Error::CircularImport {
    80	                  current: current.path,
    81	                  import,
    82	                });
    83	              }
    84	              *absolute = Some(import.clone());
    85	              stack.push(current.import(import, path.offset));
    86	            } else if !*optional {
    87	              return Err(Error::MissingImportFile { path: *path });
    88	            }
    89	          }
    90	          _ => {}
    91	        }
    92	      }
    93	
    94	      asts.insert(current.path, ast.clone());
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    let justfile = Analyzer::analyze(&asts, None, &[], &loaded, None, &paths, root)?;
    98	
    99	    Ok(Compilation {
   100	      asts,
   101	      justfile,
   102	      root: root.into(),
   103	      srcs,
   104	    })
   105	  }
   106	
   107	  fn find_module_file<'src>(
   108	    parent: &Path,
   109	    module: Name<'src>,
   110	    path: Option<&Path>,
   111	  ) -> RunResult<'src, Option<PathBuf>> {
   112	    let mut candidates = Vec::new();
   113	
   114	    if let Some(path) = path {
   115	      let full = parent.join(path);
   116	
   117	      if full.is_file() {
   118	        return Ok(Some(full));
   119	      }
   120	
   121	      candidates.push((path.join("mod.just"), true));
   122	
   123	      for name in search::JUSTFILE_NAMES {
   124	        candidates.push((path.join(name), false));
   125	      }
   126	    } else {
   127	      candidates.push((format!("{module}.just").into(), true));
   128	      candidates.push((format!("{module}/mod.just").into(), true));
   129	
   130	      for name in search::JUSTFILE_NAMES {
   131	        candidates.push((format!("{module}/{name}").into(), false));
   132	      }
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    let mut grouped = BTreeMap::<PathBuf, Vec<(PathBuf, bool)>>::new();
   136	
   137	    for (candidate, case_sensitive) in candidates {
   138	      let candidate = parent.join(candidate).lexiclean();
   139	      grouped
   140	        .entry(candidate.parent().unwrap().into())
   141	        .or_default()
   142	        .push((candidate, case_sensitive));
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    let mut found = Vec::new();
   146	
   147	    for (directory, candidates) in grouped {
   148	      let entries = match fs::read_dir(&directory) {
   149	        Ok(entries) => entries,
   150	        Err(io_error) => {
   151	          if io_error.kind() == io::ErrorKind::NotFound {
   152	            continue;
   153	          }
   154	
   155	          return Err(
   156	            SearchError::Io {
   157	              io_error,
   158	              directory,
   159	            }
   160	            .into(),
   161	          );
   162	        }
   163	      };
   164	
   165	      for entry in entries {
   166	        let entry = entry.map_err(|io_error| SearchError::Io {
   167	          io_error,
   168	          directory: directory.clone(),
   169	        })?;
   170	
   171	        if let Some(name) = entry.file_name().to_str() {
   172	          for (candidate, case_sensitive) in &candidates {
   173	            let candidate_name = candidate.file_name().unwrap().to_str().unwrap();
   174	
   175	            let eq = if *case_sensitive {
   176	              name == candidate_name
   177	            } else {
   178	              name.eq_ignore_ascii_case(candidate_name)
   179	            };
   180	
   181	            if eq {
   182	              found.push(candidate.parent().unwrap().join(name));
   183	            }
   184	          }
   185	        }
   186	      }
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    if found.len() > 1 {
   190	      found.sort();
   191	      Err(Error::AmbiguousModuleFile {
   192	        found: found
   193	          .into_iter()
   194	          .map(|found| found.strip_prefix(parent).unwrap().into())
   195	          .collect(),
   196	        module,
   197	      })
   198	    } else {
   199	      Ok(found.into_iter().next())
   200	    }
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  fn expand_tilde(path: &str) -> RunResult<'static, PathBuf> {
   204	    Ok(if let Some(path) = path.strip_prefix("~/") {
   205	      dirs::home_dir()
   206	        .ok_or(Error::Homedir)?
   207	        .join(path.trim_start_matches('/'))
   208	    } else {
   209	      PathBuf::from(path)
   210	    })
   211	  }

   291	      let module = Name {
   292	        token: Token {
   293	          column: 0,
   294	          kind: TokenKind::Identifier,
   295	          length: 3,
   296	          line: 0,
   297	          offset: 0,

   299	          src: "foo",
   300	        },
   301	      };
   302	
   303	      let tempdir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();
   304	
   305	      for file in files {
   306	        if let Some(parent) = Path::new(file).parent() {
   307	          fs::create_dir_all(tempdir.path().join(parent)).unwrap();
   308	        }
   309	
   310	        fs::write(tempdir.path().join(file), "").unwrap();
   311	      }

   313	      let actual = Compiler::find_module_file(tempdir.path(), module, path.map(Path::new));
   314	
   315	      match expected {

   317	          Error::AmbiguousModuleFile { found, .. } => {

    13	impl<'src> Source<'src> {
    14	  pub(crate) fn root(path: &Path) -> Self {
    15	    Self {
    16	      file_depth: 0,
    17	      file_path: vec![path.into()],
    18	      import_offsets: Vec::new(),
    19	      namepath: None,
    20	      path: path.into(),
    21	      working_directory: path.parent().unwrap().into(),
    22	    }
    23	  }
    24	
    25	  pub(crate) fn import(&self, path: PathBuf, import_offset: usize) -> Self {
    26	    Self {
    27	      file_depth: self.file_depth + 1,
    28	      file_path: self
    29	        .file_path
    30	        .clone()
    31	        .into_iter()
    32	        .chain(iter::once(path.clone()))
    33	        .collect(),
    34	      import_offsets: self
    35	        .import_offsets
    36	        .iter()
    37	        .copied()
    38	        .chain(iter::once(import_offset))
    39	        .collect(),
    40	      namepath: self.namepath.clone(),
    41	      path,
    42	      working_directory: self.working_directory.clone(),
    43	    }
    44	  }

    49	      file_path: self
    50	        .file_path
    51	        .clone()
    52	        .into_iter()
    53	        .chain(iter::once(path.clone()))
    54	        .collect(),

    59	          .as_ref()

     2	
     3	/// The top-level type produced by the parser. Not all successful parses result
     4	/// in valid justfiles, so additional consistency checks and name resolution
     5	/// are performed by the `Analyzer`, which produces a `Justfile` from an `Ast`.
     6	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
     7	pub(crate) struct Ast<'src> {
     8	  pub(crate) items: Vec<Item<'src>>,
     9	  pub(crate) module_path: String,
    10	  pub(crate) unstable_features: BTreeSet<UnstableFeature>,
    11	  pub(crate) warnings: Vec<Warning>,
    12	  pub(crate) working_directory: PathBuf,
    13	}
    14	
    15	impl Display for Ast<'_> {
    16	  fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
    17	    let mut iter = self.items.iter().peekable();
    18	
    19	    while let Some(item) = iter.next() {
    20	      writeln!(f, "{item}")?;
    21	
    22	      if let Some(next_item) = iter.peek() {
    23	        if matches!(item, Item::Recipe(_))
    24	          || mem::discriminant(item) != mem::discriminant(next_item)
    25	        {
    26	          writeln!(f)?;
    27	        }
    28	      }
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    Ok(())
    32	  }
    33	}

     4	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
     5	pub(crate) enum Item<'src> {
     6	  Alias(Alias<'src, Namepath<'src>>),
     7	  Assignment(Assignment<'src>),
     8	  Comment(&'src str),
     9	  Import {

    14	  },

    21	    relative: Option<StringLiteral<'src>>,
    22	  },
    23	  Recipe(UnresolvedRecipe<'src>),
    24	  Set(Set<'src>),
    25	  Unexport {
    26	    name: Name<'src>,
    27	  },
    28	}
    29	
    30	impl Display for Item<'_> {
    31	  fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
    32	    match self {
    33	      Self::Alias(alias) => write!(f, "{alias}"),
    34	      Self::Assignment(assignment) => write!(f, "{assignment}"),
    35	      Self::Comment(comment) => write!(f, "{comment}"),
    36	      Self::Import {
    37	        relative, optional, ..
    38	      } => {
    39	        write!(f, "import")?;
    40	
    41	        if *optional {
    42	          write!(f, "?")?;
    43	        }
    44	
    45	        write!(f, " {relative}")
    46	      }
    47	      Self::Module {
    48	        name,
    49	        relative,
    50	        optional,
    51	        ..
    52	      } => {
    53	        write!(f, "mod")?;
    54	
    55	        if *optional {
    56	          write!(f, "?")?;
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        write!(f, " {name}")?;
    60	
    61	        if let Some(path) = relative {
    62	          write!(f, " {path}")?;
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        Ok(())
    66	      }
    67	      Self::Recipe(recipe) => write!(f, "{}", recipe.color_display(Color::never())),
    68	      Self::Set(set) => write!(f, "{set}"),
    69	      Self::Unexport { name } => write!(f, "unexport {name}"),

     1	use super::*;
     2	
     3	pub(crate) struct Evaluator<'src: 'run, 'run> {
     4	  pub(crate) assignments: Option<&'run Table<'src, Assignment<'src>>>,
     5	  pub(crate) context: ExecutionContext<'src, 'run>,
     6	  pub(crate) is_dependency: bool,
     7	  pub(crate) scope: Scope<'src, 'run>,
     8	}
     9	
    10	impl<'src, 'run> Evaluator<'src, 'run> {
    11	  pub(crate) fn evaluate_assignments(
    12	    config: &'run Config,
    13	    dotenv: &'run BTreeMap<String, String>,
    14	    module: &'run Justfile<'src>,
    15	    overrides: &BTreeMap<String, String>,
    16	    parent: &'run Scope<'src, 'run>,
    17	    search: &'run Search,
    18	  ) -> RunResult<'src, Scope<'src, 'run>>
    19	  where
    20	    'src: 'run,
    21	  {
    22	    let context = ExecutionContext {
    23	      config,
    24	      dotenv,
    25	      module,
    26	      search,
    27	    };
    28	
    29	    let mut scope = parent.child();
    30	    let mut unknown_overrides = Vec::new();
    31	
    32	    for (name, value) in overrides {
    33	      if let Some(assignment) = module.assignments.get(name) {
    34	        scope.bind(Binding {
    35	          constant: false,
    36	          export: assignment.export,
    37	          file_depth: 0,
    38	          name: assignment.name,
    39	          private: assignment.private,
    40	          value: value.clone(),
    41	        });
    42	      } else {
    43	        unknown_overrides.push(name.clone());
    44	      }
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    if !unknown_overrides.is_empty() {
    48	      return Err(Error::UnknownOverrides {
    49	        overrides: unknown_overrides,
    50	      });
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    let mut evaluator = Self {
    54	      context,
    55	      assignments: Some(&module.assignments),
    56	      scope,
    57	      is_dependency: false,
    58	    };
    59	
    60	    for assignment in module.assignments.values() {
    61	      evaluator.evaluate_assignment(assignment)?;
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    Ok(evaluator.scope)
    65	  }
    66	
    67	  fn evaluate_assignment(&mut self, assignment: &Assignment<'src>) -> RunResult<'src, &str> {
    68	    let name = assignment.name.lexeme();
    69	
    70	    if !self.scope.bound(name) {
    71	      let value = self.evaluate_expression(&assignment.value)?;
    72	      self.scope.bind(Binding {
    73	        constant: false,
    74	        export: assignment.export,
    75	        file_depth: 0,
    76	        name: assignment.name,
    77	        private: assignment.private,
    78	        value,
    79	      });
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    Ok(self.scope.value(name).unwrap())
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  pub(crate) fn evaluate_expression(
    86	    &mut self,
    87	    expression: &Expression<'src>,
    88	  ) -> RunResult<'src, String> {
    89	    match expression {
    90	      Expression::And { lhs, rhs } => {
    91	        let lhs = self.evaluate_expression(lhs)?;
    92	        if lhs.is_empty() {
    93	          return Ok(String::new());
    94	        }
    95	        self.evaluate_expression(rhs)
    96	      }
    97	      Expression::Assert { condition, error } => {
    98	        if self.evaluate_condition(condition)? {
    99	          Ok(String::new())
   100	        } else {
   101	          Err(Error::Assert {
   102	            message: self.evaluate_expression(error)?,
   103	          })
   104	        }
   105	      }
   106	      Expression::Backtick { contents, token } => {
   107	        if self.context.config.dry_run {
   108	          Ok(format!("`{contents}`"))
   109	        } else {
   110	          Ok(self.run_backtick(contents, token)?)
   111	        }
   112	      }
   113	      Expression::Call { thunk } => {
   114	        use Thunk::*;
   115	        let result = match thunk {
   116	          Nullary { function, .. } => function(function::Context::new(self, thunk.name())),
   117	          Unary { function, arg, .. } => {
   118	            let arg = self.evaluate_expression(arg)?;
   119	            function(function::Context::new(self, thunk.name()), &arg)
   120	          }
   121	          UnaryOpt {
   122	            function,
   123	            args: (a, b),
   124	            ..
   125	          } => {
   126	            let a = self.evaluate_expression(a)?;
   127	            let b = match b.as_ref() {
   128	              Some(b) => Some(self.evaluate_expression(b)?),
   129	              None => None,
   130	            };
   131	            function(function::Context::new(self, thunk.name()), &a, b.as_deref())
   132	          }
   133	          UnaryPlus {
   134	            function,
   135	            args: (a, rest),
   136	            ..
   137	          } => {
   138	            let a = self.evaluate_expression(a)?;
   139	            let mut rest_evaluated = Vec::new();
   140	            for arg in rest {
   141	              rest_evaluated.push(self.evaluate_expression(arg)?);
   142	            }
   143	            function(
   144	              function::Context::new(self, thunk.name()),
   145	              &a,
   146	              &rest_evaluated,
   147	            )
   148	          }
   149	          Binary {
   150	            function,
   151	            args: [a, b],
   152	            ..
   153	          } => {
   154	            let a = self.evaluate_expression(a)?;
   155	            let b = self.evaluate_expression(b)?;
   156	            function(function::Context::new(self, thunk.name()), &a, &b)
   157	          }
   158	          BinaryPlus {
   159	            function,
   160	            args: ([a, b], rest),
   161	            ..
   162	          } => {
   163	            let a = self.evaluate_expression(a)?;
   164	            let b = self.evaluate_expression(b)?;
   165	            let mut rest_evaluated = Vec::new();
   166	            for arg in rest {
   167	              rest_evaluated.push(self.evaluate_expression(arg)?);
   168	            }
   169	            function(
   170	              function::Context::new(self, thunk.name()),
   171	              &a,
   172	              &b,
   173	              &rest_evaluated,
   174	            )
   175	          }
   176	          Ternary {
   177	            function,
   178	            args: [a, b, c],
   179	            ..
   180	          } => {
   181	            let a = self.evaluate_expression(a)?;
   182	            let b = self.evaluate_expression(b)?;
   183	            let c = self.evaluate_expression(c)?;
   184	            function(function::Context::new(self, thunk.name()), &a, &b, &c)
   185	          }
   186	        };
   187	        result.map_err(|message| Error::FunctionCall {
   188	          function: thunk.name(),
   189	          message,
   190	        })
   191	      }
   192	      Expression::Concatenation { lhs, rhs } => {
   193	        let lhs = self.evaluate_expression(lhs)?;
   194	        let rhs = self.evaluate_expression(rhs)?;
   195	        Ok(lhs + &rhs)
   196	      }
   197	      Expression::Conditional {
   198	        condition,
   199	        then,
   200	        otherwise,
   201	      } => {
   202	        if self.evaluate_condition(condition)? {
   203	          self.evaluate_expression(then)
   204	        } else {
   205	          self.evaluate_expression(otherwise)
   206	        }
   207	      }
   208	      Expression::Group { contents } => self.evaluate_expression(contents),
   209	      Expression::Join { lhs: None, rhs } => Ok("/".to_string() + &self.evaluate_expression(rhs)?),
   210	      Expression::Join {
   211	        lhs: Some(lhs),
   212	        rhs,
   213	      } => {
   214	        let lhs = self.evaluate_expression(lhs)?;
   215	        let rhs = self.evaluate_expression(rhs)?;
   216	        Ok(lhs + "/" + &rhs)
   217	      }
   218	      Expression::Or { lhs, rhs } => {
   219	        let lhs = self.evaluate_expression(lhs)?;
   220	        if !lhs.is_empty() {
   221	          return Ok(lhs);
   222	        }
   223	        self.evaluate_expression(rhs)
   224	      }
   225	      Expression::StringLiteral { string_literal } => Ok(string_literal.cooked.clone()),
   226	      Expression::Variable { name, .. } => {
   227	        let variable = name.lexeme();
   228	        if let Some(value) = self.scope.value(variable) {
   229	          Ok(value.to_owned())
   230	        } else if let Some(assignment) = self
   231	          .assignments
   232	          .and_then(|assignments| assignments.get(variable))
   233	        {
   234	          Ok(self.evaluate_assignment(assignment)?.to_owned())
   235	        } else {
   236	          Err(Error::Internal {
   237	            message: format!("attempted to evaluate undefined variable `{variable}`"),
   238	          })
   239	        }
   240	      }
   241	    }
   242	  }
   243	
   244	  fn evaluate_condition(&mut self, condition: &Condition<'src>) -> RunResult<'src, bool> {
   245	    let lhs_value = self.evaluate_expression(&condition.lhs)?;
   246	    let rhs_value = self.evaluate_expression(&condition.rhs)?;
   247	    let condition = match condition.operator {
   248	      ConditionalOperator::Equality => lhs_value == rhs_value,
   249	      ConditionalOperator::Inequality => lhs_value != rhs_value,
   250	      ConditionalOperator::RegexMatch => Regex::new(&rhs_value)
   251	        .map_err(|source| Error::RegexCompile { source })?
   252	        .is_match(&lhs_value),
   253	      ConditionalOperator::RegexMismatch => !Regex::new(&rhs_value)
   254	        .map_err(|source| Error::RegexCompile { source })?
   255	        .is_match(&lhs_value),
   256	    };
   257	    Ok(condition)
   258	  }
   259	
   260	  fn run_backtick(&self, raw: &str, token: &Token<'src>) -> RunResult<'src, String> {
   261	    self
   262	      .run_command(raw, &[])
   263	      .map_err(|output_error| Error::Backtick {
   264	        token: *token,
   265	        output_error,
   266	      })
   267	  }
   268	
   269	  pub(crate) fn run_command(&self, command: &str, args: &[&str]) -> Result<String, OutputError> {
   270	    let mut cmd = self
   271	      .context
   272	      .module
   273	      .settings
   274	      .shell_command(self.context.config);
   275	
   276	    cmd
   277	      .arg(command)
   278	      .args(args)
   279	      .current_dir(self.context.working_directory())
   280	      .export(
   281	        &self.context.module.settings,
   282	        self.context.dotenv,
   283	        &self.scope,
   284	        &self.context.module.unexports,
   285	      )
   286	      .stdin(Stdio::inherit())
   287	      .stderr(if self.context.config.verbosity.quiet() {
   288	        Stdio::null()
   289	      } else {
   290	        Stdio::inherit()
   291	      })
   292	      .stdout(Stdio::piped());
   293	
   294	    cmd.output_guard_stdout()
   295	  }
   296	
   297	  pub(crate) fn evaluate_line(
   298	    &mut self,
   299	    line: &Line<'src>,
   300	    continued: bool,
   301	  ) -> RunResult<'src, String> {
   302	    let mut evaluated = String::new();
   303	    for (i, fragment) in line.fragments.iter().enumerate() {
   304	      match fragment {
   305	        Fragment::Text { token } => {
   306	          let lexeme = token.lexeme().replace("{{{{", "{{");
   307	
   308	          if i == 0 && continued {
   309	            evaluated += lexeme.trim_start();
   310	          } else {
   311	            evaluated += &lexeme;
   312	          }
   313	        }
   314	        Fragment::Interpolation { expression } => {
   315	          evaluated += &self.evaluate_expression(expression)?;
   316	        }
   317	      }
   318	    }
   319	    Ok(evaluated)
   320	  }
   321	
   322	  pub(crate) fn evaluate_parameters(
   323	    context: &ExecutionContext<'src, 'run>,
   324	    is_dependency: bool,
   325	    arguments: &[String],
   326	    parameters: &[Parameter<'src>],
   327	    scope: &'run Scope<'src, 'run>,
   328	  ) -> RunResult<'src, (Scope<'src, 'run>, Vec<String>)> {
   329	    let mut evaluator = Self::new(context, is_dependency, scope);
   330	
   331	    let mut positional = Vec::new();
   332	
   333	    let mut rest = arguments;
   334	    for parameter in parameters {
   335	      let value = if rest.is_empty() {
   336	        if let Some(ref default) = parameter.default {
   337	          let value = evaluator.evaluate_expression(default)?;
   338	          positional.push(value.clone());
   339	          value
   340	        } else if parameter.kind == ParameterKind::Star {
   341	          String::new()
   342	        } else {
   343	          return Err(Error::Internal {
   344	            message: "missing parameter without default".to_owned(),
   345	          });
   346	        }
   347	      } else if parameter.kind.is_variadic() {
   348	        for value in rest {
   349	          positional.push(value.clone());
   350	        }
   351	        let value = rest.to_vec().join(" ");
   352	        rest = &[];
   353	        value
   354	      } else {
   355	        let value = rest[0].clone();
   356	        positional.push(value.clone());
   357	        rest = &rest[1..];
   358	        value
   359	      };
   360	      evaluator.scope.bind(Binding {
   361	        constant: false,
   362	        export: parameter.export,
   363	        file_depth: 0,
   364	        name: parameter.name,
   365	        private: false,
   366	        value,
   367	      });
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    Ok((evaluator.scope, positional))
   371	  }
   372	
   373	  pub(crate) fn new(
   374	    context: &ExecutionContext<'src, 'run>,
   375	    is_dependency: bool,
   376	    scope: &'run Scope<'src, 'run>,
   377	  ) -> Self {
   378	    Self {
   379	      assignments: None,
   380	      context: *context,
   381	      is_dependency,
   382	      scope: scope.child(),
   383	    }
   384	  }
   385	}

     4	  assignments: &'run Table<'src, Assignment<'src>>,
     5	  modules: &'run Table<'src, Justfile<'src>>,
     6	  resolved_recipes: Table<'src, Arc<Recipe<'src>>>,
     7	  unresolved_recipes: Table<'src, UnresolvedRecipe<'src>>,
     8	}
     9	
    10	impl<'src: 'run, 'run> RecipeResolver<'src, 'run> {
    11	  pub(crate) fn resolve_recipes(
    12	    assignments: &'run Table<'src, Assignment<'src>>,
    13	    modules: &'run Table<'src, Justfile<'src>>,
    14	    settings: &Settings,
    15	    unresolved_recipes: Table<'src, UnresolvedRecipe<'src>>,
    16	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Table<'src, Arc<Recipe<'src>>>> {
    17	    let mut resolver = Self {
    18	      resolved_recipes: Table::new(),
    19	      unresolved_recipes,
    20	      assignments,
    21	      modules,
    22	    };
    23	
    24	    while let Some(unresolved) = resolver.unresolved_recipes.pop() {
    25	      resolver.resolve_recipe(&mut Vec::new(), unresolved)?;
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    for recipe in resolver.resolved_recipes.values() {
    29	      for (i, parameter) in recipe.parameters.iter().enumerate() {
    30	        if let Some(expression) = &parameter.default {
    31	          for variable in expression.variables() {
    32	            resolver.resolve_variable(&variable, &recipe.parameters[..i])?;
    33	          }
    34	        }
    35	      }
    36	
    37	      for dependency in &recipe.dependencies {
    38	        for argument in &dependency.arguments {
    39	          for variable in argument.variables() {
    40	            resolver.resolve_variable(&variable, &recipe.parameters)?;
    41	          }
    42	        }
    43	      }
    44	
    45	      for line in &recipe.body {
    46	        if line.is_comment() && settings.ignore_comments {
    47	          continue;
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        for fragment in &line.fragments {
    51	          if let Fragment::Interpolation { expression, .. } = fragment {
    52	            for variable in expression.variables() {
    53	              resolver.resolve_variable(&variable, &recipe.parameters)?;
    54	            }
    55	          }
    56	        }
    57	      }
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    Ok(resolver.resolved_recipes)
    61	  }
    62	
    63	  fn resolve_variable(
    64	    &self,
    65	    variable: &Token<'src>,
    66	    parameters: &[Parameter],
    67	  ) -> CompileResult<'src> {
    68	    let name = variable.lexeme();
    69	
    70	    let defined = self.assignments.contains_key(name)
    71	      || parameters.iter().any(|p| p.name.lexeme() == name)
    72	      || constants().contains_key(name);
    73	
    74	    if !defined {
    75	      return Err(variable.error(UndefinedVariable { variable: name }));
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    Ok(())
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  fn resolve_recipe(
    82	    &mut self,
    83	    stack: &mut Vec<&'src str>,
    84	    recipe: UnresolvedRecipe<'src>,
    85	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Arc<Recipe<'src>>> {
    86	    if let Some(resolved) = self.resolved_recipes.get(recipe.name()) {
    87	      return Ok(Arc::clone(resolved));
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    stack.push(recipe.name());
    91	
    92	    let dependencies = recipe
    93	      .dependencies
    94	      .iter()
    95	      .map(|dependency| {
    96	        self
    97	          .resolve_dependency(dependency, &recipe, stack)?
    98	          .ok_or_else(|| {
    99	            dependency.recipe.last().error(UnknownDependency {
   100	              recipe: recipe.name(),
   101	              unknown: dependency.recipe.clone(),
   102	            })
   103	          })
   104	      })
   105	      .collect::<CompileResult<Vec<Arc<Recipe>>>>()?;
   106	
   107	    stack.pop();
   108	
   109	    let resolved = Arc::new(recipe.resolve(dependencies)?);
   110	    self.resolved_recipes.insert(Arc::clone(&resolved));
   111	    Ok(resolved)
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  fn resolve_dependency(
   115	    &mut self,
   116	    dependency: &UnresolvedDependency<'src>,
   117	    recipe: &UnresolvedRecipe<'src>,
   118	    stack: &mut Vec<&'src str>,
   119	  ) -> CompileResult<'src, Option<Arc<Recipe<'src>>>> {
   120	    let name = dependency.recipe.last().lexeme();
   121	
   122	    if dependency.recipe.components() > 1 {
   123	      // recipe is in a submodule and is thus already resovled
   124	      Ok(Analyzer::resolve_recipe(
   125	        &dependency.recipe,
   126	        self.modules,
   127	        &self.resolved_recipes,
   128	      ))
   129	    } else if let Some(resolved) = self.resolved_recipes.get(name) {
   130	      // recipe is the current module and has already been resolved
   131	      Ok(Some(Arc::clone(resolved)))
   132	    } else if stack.contains(&name) {
   133	      // recipe depends on itself
   134	      let first = stack[0];
   135	      stack.push(first);
   136	      return Err(
   137	        dependency.recipe.last().error(CircularRecipeDependency {
   138	          recipe: recipe.name(),
   139	          circle: stack
   140	            .iter()
   141	            .skip_while(|name| **name != dependency.recipe.last().lexeme())
   142	            .copied()
   143	            .collect(),
   144	        }),
   145	      );
   146	    } else if let Some(unresolved) = self.unresolved_recipes.remove(name) {
   147	      // recipe is as of yet unresolved
   148	      Ok(Some(self.resolve_recipe(stack, unresolved)?))
   149	    } else {
   150	      // recipe is unknown
   151	      Ok(None)
   152	    }
   153	  }
   154	}

     1	use super::*;
     2	
     3	/// An expression. Note that the Just language grammar has both an `expression`
     4	/// production of additions (`a + b`) and values, and a `value` production of
     5	/// all other value types (for example strings, function calls, and
     6	/// parenthetical groups).
     7	///
     8	/// The parser parses both values and expressions into `Expression`s.
     9	#[derive(PartialEq, Debug, Clone)]
    10	pub(crate) enum Expression<'src> {
    11	  /// `lhs && rhs`
    12	  And {
    13	    lhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    14	    rhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    15	  },
    16	  /// `assert(condition, error)`
    17	  Assert {
    18	    condition: Condition<'src>,
    19	    error: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    20	  },
    21	  /// `contents`
    22	  Backtick {
    23	    contents: String,
    24	    token: Token<'src>,
    25	  },
    26	  /// `name(arguments)`
    27	  Call { thunk: Thunk<'src> },
    28	  /// `lhs + rhs`
    29	  Concatenation {
    30	    lhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    31	    rhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    32	  },
    33	  /// `if condition { then } else { otherwise }`
    34	  Conditional {
    35	    condition: Condition<'src>,
    36	    then: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    37	    otherwise: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    38	  },
    39	  /// `(contents)`
    40	  Group { contents: Box<Expression<'src>> },
    41	  /// `lhs / rhs`
    42	  Join {
    43	    lhs: Option<Box<Expression<'src>>>,
    44	    rhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    45	  },
    46	  /// `lhs || rhs`
    47	  Or {
    48	    lhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    49	    rhs: Box<Expression<'src>>,
    50	  },
    51	  /// `"string_literal"` or `'string_literal'`
    52	  StringLiteral { string_literal: StringLiteral<'src> },
    53	  /// `variable`
    54	  Variable { name: Name<'src> },
    55	}
    56	
    57	impl<'src> Expression<'src> {
    58	  pub(crate) fn variables<'expression>(&'expression self) -> Variables<'expression, 'src> {
    59	    Variables::new(self)
    60	  }
    61	}
    62	
    63	impl Display for Expression<'_> {
    64	  fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
    65	    match self {
    66	      Self::And { lhs, rhs } => write!(f, "{lhs} && {rhs}"),
    67	      Self::Assert { condition, error } => write!(f, "assert({condition}, {error})"),
    68	      Self::Backtick { token, .. } => write!(f, "{}", token.lexeme()),
    69	      Self::Call { thunk } => write!(f, "{thunk}"),
    70	      Self::Concatenation { lhs, rhs } => write!(f, "{lhs} + {rhs}"),
    71	      Self::Conditional {
    72	        condition,
    73	        then,
    74	        otherwise,
    75	      } => {
    76	        if let Self::Conditional { .. } = **otherwise {
    77	          write!(f, "if {condition} {{ {then} }} else {otherwise}")
    78	        } else {
    79	          write!(f, "if {condition} {{ {then} }} else {{ {otherwise} }}")
    80	        }
    81	      }
    82	      Self::Group { contents } => write!(f, "({contents})"),
    83	      Self::Join { lhs: None, rhs } => write!(f, "/ {rhs}"),
    84	      Self::Join {
    85	        lhs: Some(lhs),
    86	        rhs,
    87	      } => write!(f, "{lhs} / {rhs}"),
    88	      Self::Or { lhs, rhs } => write!(f, "{lhs} || {rhs}"),
    89	      Self::StringLiteral { string_literal } => write!(f, "{string_literal}"),
    90	      Self::Variable { name } => write!(f, "{}", name.lexeme()),
    91	    }
    92	  }
    93	}
    94	
    95	impl Serialize for Expression<'_> {
    96	  fn serialize<S>(&self, serializer: S) -> Result<S::Ok, S::Error>
    97	  where
    98	    S: Serializer,
    99	  {
   100	    match self {
   101	      Self::And { lhs, rhs } => {
   102	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   103	        seq.serialize_element("and")?;
   104	        seq.serialize_element(lhs)?;
   105	        seq.serialize_element(rhs)?;
   106	        seq.end()
   107	      }
   108	      Self::Assert { condition, error } => {
   109	        let mut seq: <S as Serializer>::SerializeSeq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   110	        seq.serialize_element("assert")?;
   111	        seq.serialize_element(condition)?;
   112	        seq.serialize_element(error)?;
   113	        seq.end()
   114	      }
   115	      Self::Backtick { contents, .. } => {
   116	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   117	        seq.serialize_element("evaluate")?;
   118	        seq.serialize_element(contents)?;
   119	        seq.end()
   120	      }
   121	      Self::Call { thunk } => thunk.serialize(serializer),
   122	      Self::Concatenation { lhs, rhs } => {
   123	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   124	        seq.serialize_element("concatenate")?;
   125	        seq.serialize_element(lhs)?;
   126	        seq.serialize_element(rhs)?;
   127	        seq.end()
   128	      }
   129	      Self::Conditional {
   130	        condition,
   131	        then,
   132	        otherwise,
   133	      } => {
   134	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   135	        seq.serialize_element("if")?;
   136	        seq.serialize_element(condition)?;
   137	        seq.serialize_element(then)?;
   138	        seq.serialize_element(otherwise)?;
   139	        seq.end()
   140	      }
   141	      Self::Group { contents } => contents.serialize(serializer),
   142	      Self::Join { lhs, rhs } => {
   143	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   144	        seq.serialize_element("join")?;
   145	        seq.serialize_element(lhs)?;
   146	        seq.serialize_element(rhs)?;
   147	        seq.end()
   148	      }
   149	      Self::Or { lhs, rhs } => {
   150	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   151	        seq.serialize_element("or")?;
   152	        seq.serialize_element(lhs)?;
   153	        seq.serialize_element(rhs)?;
   154	        seq.end()
   155	      }
   156	      Self::StringLiteral { string_literal } => string_literal.serialize(serializer),
   157	      Self::Variable { name } => {
   158	        let mut seq = serializer.serialize_seq(None)?;
   159	        seq.serialize_element("variable")?;
   160	        seq.serialize_element(name)?;
   161	        seq.end()
   162	      }
   163	    }
   164	  }
   165	}
   166

    14	  type Item = Token<'src>;
    15	
    16	  fn next(&mut self) -> Option<Token<'src>> {
    17	    loop {
    18	      match self.stack.pop()? {
    19	        Expression::And { lhs, rhs } | Expression::Or { lhs, rhs } => {
    20	          self.stack.push(lhs);
    21	          self.stack.push(rhs);
    22	        }
    23	        Expression::Assert {
    24	          condition:
    25	            Condition {
    26	              lhs,
    27	              rhs,
    28	              operator: _,
    29	            },
    30	          error,
    31	        } => {
    32	          self.stack.push(error);
    33	          self.stack.push(rhs);
    34	          self.stack.push(lhs);
    35	        }
    36	        Expression::Backtick { .. } | Expression::StringLiteral { .. } => {}
    37	        Expression::Call { thunk } => match thunk {
    38	          Thunk::Nullary { .. } => {}
    39	          Thunk::Unary { arg, .. } => self.stack.push(arg),
    40	          Thunk::UnaryOpt {
    41	            args: (a, opt_b), ..
    42	          } => {
    43	            self.stack.push(a);
    44	            if let Some(b) = opt_b.as_ref() {
    45	              self.stack.push(b);
    46	            }
    47	          }
    48	          Thunk::UnaryPlus {
    49	            args: (a, rest), ..
    50	          } => {
    51	            let first: &[&Expression] = &[a];
    52	            for arg in first.iter().copied().chain(rest).rev() {
    53	              self.stack.push(arg);
    54	            }
    55	          }
    56	          Thunk::Binary { args, .. } => {
    57	            for arg in args.iter().rev() {
    58	              self.stack.push(arg);
    59	            }
    60	          }
    61	          Thunk::BinaryPlus {
    62	            args: ([a, b], rest),
    63	            ..
    64	          } => {
    65	            let first: &[&Expression] = &[a, b];
    66	            for arg in first.iter().copied().chain(rest).rev() {
    67	              self.stack.push(arg);
    68	            }
    69	          }
    70	          Thunk::Ternary { args, .. } => {
    71	            for arg in args.iter().rev() {
    72	              self.stack.push(arg);
    73	            }
    74	          }
    75	        },
    76	        Expression::Concatenation { lhs, rhs } => {
    77	          self.stack.push(rhs);
    78	          self.stack.push(lhs);

    36	  fn find_suggestion(
    37	    input: &str,
    38	    candidates: impl Iterator<Item = Suggestion<'src>>,
    39	  ) -> Option<Suggestion<'src>> {
    40	    candidates
    41	      .map(|suggestion| (edit_distance(input, suggestion.name), suggestion))
    42	      .filter(|(distance, _suggestion)| *distance < 3)
    43	      .min_by_key(|(distance, _suggestion)| *distance)
    44	      .map(|(_distance, suggestion)| suggestion)
    45	  }
    46	
    47	  pub(crate) fn suggest_recipe(&self, input: &str) -> Option<Suggestion<'src>> {
    48	    Self::find_suggestion(
    49	      input,
    50	      self
    51	        .recipes

    53	        .map(|name| Suggestion { name, target: None })

    57	        })),
    58	    )
    59	  }

    72	    &'run self,
    73	    arena: &'run Arena<Scope<'src, 'run>>,
    74	    config: &'run Config,

    84	    scopes.insert(self.module_path.clone(), (self, scope));

   100	
   101	  pub(crate) fn run(
   102	    &self,
   103	    config: &Config,
   104	    search: &Search,
   105	    overrides: &BTreeMap<String, String>,
   106	    arguments: &[String],
   107	  ) -> RunResult<'src> {
   108	    let unknown_overrides = overrides
   109	      .keys()
   110	      .filter(|name| !self.assignments.contains_key(name.as_str()))
   111	      .cloned()
   112	      .collect::<Vec<String>>();
   113	
   114	    if !unknown_overrides.is_empty() {
   115	      return Err(Error::UnknownOverrides {
   116	        overrides: unknown_overrides,
   117	      });
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    let dotenv = if config.load_dotenv {
