   151	        };
   152	
   153	        command
   154	          .args(arguments)
   155	          .current_dir(&search.working_directory);
   156	
   157	        let scope = scope.child();
   158	
   159	        command.export(&self.settings, &dotenv, &scope, &self.unexports);
   160	
   161	        let (result, caught) = command.status_guard();
   162	
   163	        let status = result.map_err(|io_error| Error::CommandInvoke {
   164	          binary: binary.clone(),
   165	          arguments: arguments.clone(),
   166	          io_error,
   167	        })?;
   168	
   169	        if !status.success() {
   170	          return Err(Error::CommandStatus {
   171	            binary: binary.clone(),
   172	            arguments: arguments.clone(),
   173	            status,
   174	          });
   175	        }
   176	
   177	        if let Some(signal) = caught {
   178	          return Err(Error::Interrupted { signal });
   179	        }
   180	
   181	        return Ok(());
   182	      }
   183	      Subcommand::Evaluate { variable, .. } => {
   184	        if let Some(variable) = variable {
   185	          if let Some(value) = scope.value(variable) {
   186	            print!("{value}");
   187	          } else {
   188	            return Err(Error::EvalUnknownVariable {
   189	              suggestion: self.suggest_variable(variable),
   190	              variable: variable.clone(),
   191	            });
   192	          }
   193	        } else {
   194	          let width = scope.names().fold(0, |max, name| name.len().max(max));
   195	
   196	          for binding in scope.bindings() {
   197	            if !binding.private {
   198	              println!(
   199	                "{0:1$} := \"{2}\"",
   200	                binding.name.lexeme(),
   201	                width,
   202	                binding.value
   203	              );
   204	            }
   205	          }
   206	        }
   207	
   208	        return Ok(());
   209	      }
   210	      _ => {}
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    let arguments = arguments.iter().map(String::as_str).collect::<Vec<&str>>();
   214	
   215	    let groups = ArgumentParser::parse_arguments(self, &arguments)?;
   216	
   217	    let mut invocations = Vec::<Invocation>::new();
   218	
   219	    for group in &groups {
   220	      invocations.push(self.invocation(&group.arguments, &group.path, 0)?);
   221	    }
   222	
   223	    if config.one && invocations.len() > 1 {
   224	      return Err(Error::ExcessInvocations {
   225	        invocations: invocations.len(),
   226	      });
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    let ran = Ran::default();
   230	    for invocation in invocations {
   231	      Self::run_recipe(
   232	        &invocation
   233	          .arguments
   234	          .iter()
   235	          .copied()
   236	          .map(str::to_string)
   237	          .collect::<Vec<String>>(),
   238	        config,
   239	        &dotenv,
   240	        false,
   241	        &ran,
   242	        invocation.recipe,
   243	        &scopes,
   244	        search,
   245	      )?;
   246	    }
   247	
   248	    Ok(())
   249	  }
   250	
   251	  pub(crate) fn check_unstable(&self, config: &Config) -> RunResult<'src> {
   252	    if let Some(&unstable_feature) = self.unstable_features.iter().next() {
   253	      config.require_unstable(self, unstable_feature)?;
   254	    }
   255	
   256	    for module in self.modules.values() {
   257	      module.check_unstable(config)?;
   258	    }
   259	
   260	    Ok(())
   261	  }
   262	
   263	  pub(crate) fn get_alias(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&Alias<'src>> {
   264	    self.aliases.get(name)
   265	  }
   266	
   267	  pub(crate) fn get_recipe(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&Recipe<'src>> {
   268	    self
   269	      .recipes
   270	      .get(name)
   271	      .map(Arc::as_ref)
   272	      .or_else(|| self.aliases.get(name).map(|alias| alias.target.as_ref()))
   273	  }
   274	
   275	  fn invocation<'run>(
   276	    &'run self,
   277	    arguments: &[&'run str],
   278	    path: &'run [String],
   279	    position: usize,
   280	  ) -> RunResult<'src, Invocation<'src, 'run>> {
   281	    if position + 1 == path.len() {
   282	      let recipe = self.get_recipe(&path[position]).unwrap();
   283	      Ok(Invocation {
   284	        arguments: arguments.into(),
   285	        recipe,
   286	      })
   287	    } else {
   288	      let module = self.modules.get(&path[position]).unwrap();
   289	      module.invocation(arguments, path, position + 1)
   290	    }
   291	  }
   292	
   293	  pub(crate) fn is_submodule(&self) -> bool {
   294	    self.name.is_some()
   295	  }
   296	
   297	  pub(crate) fn name(&self) -> &'src str {
   298	    self.name.map(|name| name.lexeme()).unwrap_or_default()
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  fn run_recipe(
   302	    arguments: &[String],
   303	    config: &Config,
   304	    dotenv: &BTreeMap<String, String>,
   305	    is_dependency: bool,
   306	    ran: &Ran<'src>,
   307	    recipe: &Recipe<'src>,
   308	    scopes: &BTreeMap<String, (&Justfile<'src>, &Scope<'src, '_>)>,
   309	    search: &Search,
   310	  ) -> RunResult<'src> {
   311	    let mutex = ran.mutex(&recipe.namepath, arguments);
   312	
   313	    let mut guard = mutex.lock().unwrap();
   314	
   315	    if *guard {
   316	      return Ok(());
   317	    }
   318	
   319	    if !config.yes && !recipe.confirm()? {
   320	      return Err(Error::NotConfirmed {
   321	        recipe: recipe.name(),
   322	      });
   323	    }
   324	
   325	    let (module, scope) = scopes
   326	      .get(&recipe.module_path())
   327	      .expect("failed to retrieve scope for module");
   328	
   329	    let context = ExecutionContext {
   330	      config,
   331	      dotenv,
   332	      module,
   333	      search,
   334	    };
   335	
   336	    let (outer, positional) = Evaluator::evaluate_parameters(
   337	      &context,
   338	      is_dependency,
   339	      arguments,
   340	      &recipe.parameters,
   341	      scope,
   342	    )?;
   343	
   344	    let scope = outer.child();
   345	
   346	    let mut evaluator = Evaluator::new(&context, true, &scope);
   347	
   348	    Self::run_dependencies(
   349	      config,
   350	      &context,
   351	      recipe.priors(),
   352	      dotenv,
   353	      &mut evaluator,
   354	      ran,
   355	      recipe,
   356	      scopes,
   357	      search,
   358	    )?;
   359	
   360	    recipe.run(&context, &scope, &positional, is_dependency)?;
   361	
   362	    Self::run_dependencies(
   363	      config,
   364	      &context,
   365	      recipe.subsequents(),
   366	      dotenv,
   367	      &mut evaluator,
   368	      &Ran::default(),
   369	      recipe,
   370	      scopes,
   371	      search,
   372	    )?;
   373	
   374	    *guard = true;
   375	
   376	    Ok(())
   377	  }
   378	
   379	  fn run_dependencies<'run>(
   380	    config: &Config,
   381	    context: &ExecutionContext<'src, 'run>,
   382	    dependencies: &[Dependency<'src>],
   383	    dotenv: &BTreeMap<String, String>,
   384	    evaluator: &mut Evaluator<'src, 'run>,
   385	    ran: &Ran<'src>,
   386	    recipe: &Recipe<'src>,
   387	    scopes: &BTreeMap<String, (&Justfile<'src>, &Scope<'src, 'run>)>,
   388	    search: &Search,
   389	  ) -> RunResult<'src> {
   390	    if context.config.no_dependencies {
   391	      return Ok(());
   392	    }
   393	
   394	    let mut evaluated = Vec::new();
   395	    for Dependency { recipe, arguments } in dependencies {
   396	      let arguments = arguments
   397	        .iter()
   398	        .map(|argument| evaluator.evaluate_expression(argument))
   399	        .collect::<RunResult<Vec<String>>>()?;
   400	      evaluated.push((recipe, arguments));
   401	    }
   402	
   403	    if recipe.is_parallel() {
   404	      thread::scope::<_, RunResult>(|thread_scope| {
   405	        let mut handles = Vec::new();
   406	        for (recipe, arguments) in evaluated {
   407	          handles.push(thread_scope.spawn(move || {
   408	            Self::run_recipe(
   409	              &arguments, config, dotenv, true, ran, recipe, scopes, search,
   410	            )
   411	          }));
   412	        }
   413	        for handle in handles {
   414	          handle
   415	            .join()
   416	            .map_err(|_| Error::internal("parallel dependency thread panicked"))??;
   417	        }
   418	        Ok(())
   419	      })?;
   420	    } else {
   421	      for (recipe, arguments) in evaluated {
   422	        Self::run_recipe(
   423	          &arguments, config, dotenv, true, ran, recipe, scopes, search,
   424	        )?;
   425	      }
   426	    }
   427	
   428	    Ok(())
   429	  }
   430	
   431	  pub(crate) fn modules(&self, config: &Config) -> Vec<&Justfile> {
   432	    let mut modules = self.modules.values().collect::<Vec<&Justfile>>();
   433	
   434	    if config.unsorted {
   435	      modules.sort_by_key(|module| {
   436	        module
   437	          .name
   438	          .map(|name| name.token.offset)
   439	          .unwrap_or_default()
   440	      });
   441	    }
   442	
   443	    modules
   444	  }
   445	
   446	  pub(crate) fn public_recipes(&self, config: &Config) -> Vec<&Recipe> {
   447	    let mut recipes = self
   448	      .recipes
   449	      .values()
   450	      .map(AsRef::as_ref)
   451	      .filter(|recipe| recipe.is_public())
   452	      .collect::<Vec<&Recipe>>();
   453	
   454	    if config.unsorted {
   455	      recipes.sort_by_key(|recipe| (&recipe.import_offsets, recipe.name.offset));
   456	    }
   457	
   458	    recipes
   459	  }
   460	
   461	  pub(crate) fn groups(&self) -> &[String] {
   462	    &self.groups
   463	  }
   464	
   465	  pub(crate) fn public_groups(&self, config: &Config) -> Vec<String> {
   466	    let mut groups = Vec::new();
   467	
   468	    for recipe in self.recipes.values() {
   469	      if recipe.is_public() {
   470	        for group in recipe.groups() {
   471	          groups.push((recipe.import_offsets.as_slice(), recipe.name.offset, group));
   472	        }
   473	      }
   474	    }
   475	
   476	    for submodule in self.modules.values() {
   477	      for group in submodule.groups() {
   478	        groups.push((&[], submodule.name.unwrap().offset, group.to_string()));
   479	      }
   480	    }
   481	
   482	    if config.unsorted {
   483	      groups.sort();
   484	    } else {
   485	      groups.sort_by(|(_, _, a), (_, _, b)| a.cmp(b));
   486	    }
   487	
   488	    let mut seen = HashSet::new();
   489	
   490	    groups.retain(|(_, _, group)| seen.insert(group.clone()));
   491	
   492	    groups.into_iter().map(|(_, _, group)| group).collect()
   493	  }
   494	}
   495	
   496	impl ColorDisplay for Justfile<'_> {
   497	  fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter, color: Color) -> fmt::Result {
   498	    let mut items = self.recipes.len() + self.assignments.len() + self.aliases.len();
   499	    for (name, assignment) in &self.assignments {
   500	      if assignment.export {
   501	        write!(f, "export ")?;
   502	      }
   503	      write!(f, "{name} := {}", assignment.value)?;
   504	      items -= 1;
   505	      if items != 0 {
   506	        write!(f, "\n\n")?;
   507	      }
   508	    }
   509	    for alias in self.aliases.values() {
   510	      write!(f, "{alias}")?;
   511	      items -= 1;
   512	      if items != 0 {
   513	        write!(f, "\n\n")?;
   514	      }
   515	    }
   516	    for recipe in self.recipes.values() {
   517	      write!(f, "{}", recipe.color_display(color))?;
   518	      items -= 1;
   519	      if items != 0 {
   520	        write!(f, "\n\n")?;
   521	      }
   522	    }
   523	    Ok(())
   524	  }
   525	}
   526	
   527	impl<'src> Keyed<'src> for Justfile<'src> {
   528	  fn key(&self) -> &'src str {
   529	    self.name()
   530	  }
   531	}

     6	  pub(crate) fn compile<'src>(
     7	    loader: &'src Loader,
     8	    root: &Path,
     9	  ) -> RunResult<'src, Compilation<'src>> {
    10	    let mut asts = HashMap::<PathBuf, Ast>::new();
    11	    let mut loaded = Vec::new();
    12	    let mut paths = HashMap::<PathBuf, PathBuf>::new();
    13	    let mut srcs = HashMap::<PathBuf, &str>::new();
    14	
    15	    let mut stack = Vec::new();
    16	    stack.push(Source::root(root));
    17	
    18	    while let Some(current) = stack.pop() {
    19	      let (relative, src) = loader.load(root, &current.path)?;
    20	      loaded.push(relative.into());
    21	      let tokens = Lexer::lex(relative, src)?;
    22	      let mut ast = Parser::parse(
    23	        current.file_depth,
    24	        &current.import_offsets,
    25	        current.namepath.as_ref(),
    26	        &tokens,
    27	        &current.working_directory,
    28	      )?;
    29	
    30	      let mut items = Vec::new();
    31	
    32	      for item in ast.items {
    33	        match item {
    34	          Item::Module {
    35	            absolute,
    36	            name,
    37	            optional,
    38	            relative,
    39	            doc,
    40	            groups,
    41	          } => {
    42	            let parent = current.path.parent().unwrap();
    43

    47	              .transpose()?;

    50

    52	              if current.file_path.contains(&import) {
    53	                return Err(Error::CircularImport {
    54	                  current: current.path,
    55	                  import,
    56	                });
    57	              }

    61	                optional,

    63	                doc,

   107	          }
   108	        }
   109	      }
   110	
   111	      ast.items = items;
   112	      paths.insert(current.path.clone(), relative.into());
   113	      srcs.insert(current.path.clone(), src);

   109	        Item::Recipe(recipe) => {
   110	          if recipe.enabled() {
   111	            Self::analyze_recipe(recipe)?;
   112	            self.recipes.push(recipe);
   113	          }
   114	        }
   115	        Item::Set(set) => {
   116	          self.analyze_set(set)?;
   117	          self.sets.insert(set.clone());
   118	        }
   119	        Item::Unexport { name } => {
   120	          if !self.unexports.insert(name.lexeme().to_string()) {
   121	            return Err(name.token.error(DuplicateUnexport {
   122	              variable: name.lexeme(),
   123	            }));
   124	          }
   125	        }
   126	      }
   127	    }
   128	
   129	    let settings = Settings::from_table(self.sets);

     2	
     3	#[derive(PartialEq, Debug, Clone, Ord, Eq, PartialOrd)]
     4	pub(crate) struct StringLiteral<'src> {
     5	  pub(crate) cooked: String,
     6	  pub(crate) expand: bool,
     7	  pub(crate) kind: StringKind,
     8	  pub(crate) raw: &'src str,
     9	}
    10	
    11	impl<'src> StringLiteral<'src> {
    12	  pub(crate) fn from_raw(raw: &'src str) -> Self {
    13	    Self {
    14	      cooked: raw.into(),
    15	      expand: false,
    16	      kind: StringKind {
    17	        delimiter: StringDelimiter::QuoteSingle,
    18	        indented: false,
    19	      },
    20	      raw,
    21	    }
    22	  }
    23	}
    24	
    25	impl Display for StringLiteral<'_> {
    26	  fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter) -> fmt::Result {
    27	    if self.expand {
    28	      write!(f, "x")?;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    write!(
    32	      f,
    33	      "{}{}{}",
    34	      self.kind.delimiter(),
    35	      self.raw,
    36	      self.kind.delimiter()
    37	    )
    38	  }
    39	}
    40	
    41	impl Serialize for StringLiteral<'_> {
    42	  fn serialize<S>(&self, serializer: S) -> Result<S::Ok, S::Error>
    43	  where
    44	    S: Serializer,
    45	  {
    46	    serializer.serialize_str(&self.cooked)
    47	  }
    48	}

                stack.push(asts.get(absolute).unwrap());

    let mut definitions = HashMap::new();
    let mut imports = HashSet::new();
    let mut unstable_features = BTreeSet::new();

    let ast = asts.get(root).unwrap();
    let mut items = ast.items.iter().rev().collect::<Vec<_>>();
    unstable_features.extend(&ast.unstable_features);
    self.warnings.extend(ast.warnings.iter().cloned());
    imports.insert(root);

    while let Some(item) = items.pop() {
      match item {
        Item::Alias(alias) => {
          Self::define(&mut definitions, alias.name, "alias", false)?;
          self.aliases.insert(alias.clone());
        }
        Item::Assignment(assignment) => {
          self.assignments.push(assignment);
        }
        Item::Comment(_) => (),
        Item::Import { absolute, .. } => {
          if let Some(absolute) = absolute {
            if imports.insert(absolute) {
              let ast = asts.get(absolute).unwrap();
              unstable_features.extend(&ast.unstable_features);
              self.warnings.extend(ast.warnings.iter().cloned());
              for item in ast.items.iter().rev() {
                items.push(item);
              }
            }
          }
        }
        Item::Module {
          absolute,
          doc,
          groups,
          name,
          ..
        } => {
          if let Some(absolute) = absolute {
            Self::define(&mut definitions, *name, "module", false)?;
            self.modules.insert(Self::analyze(
              asts,
              doc.clone(),
              groups.as_slice(),
              loaded,
              Some(*name),
              paths,
              absolute,
            )?);
          }
        }
        Item::Recipe(recipe) => {
          if recipe.enabled() {
            Self::analyze_recipe(recipe)?;
            self.recipes.push(recipe);
          }
        }
        Item::Set(set) => {
          self.analyze_set(set)?;
          self.sets.insert(set.clone());
        }
        Item::Unexport { name } => {
          if !self.unexports.insert(name.lexeme().to_string()) {
            return Err(name.token.error(DuplicateUnexport {
              variable: name.lexeme(),
            }));
          }
        }
      }
    }
' --new_str '  ) -> CompileResult<'"'"'src, Justfile<'"'"'src>> {
    let mut definitions = HashMap::new();
    let mut imports = HashSet::new();
    let mut unstable_features = BTreeSet::new();

    let mut stack = Vec::new();
    let ast = asts.get(root).unwrap();
    stack.push(ast);

    while let Some(ast) = stack.pop() {
      unstable_features.extend(&ast.unstable_features);

      for item in ast.items.iter().rev() {
        match item {
          Item::Alias(alias) => {
            Self::define(&mut definitions, alias.name, "alias", false)?;
            self.aliases.insert(alias.clone());
          }
          Item::Assignment(assignment) => {
            self.assignments.push(assignment);
          }
          Item::Comment(_) => (),
          Item::Import { absolute, .. } => {
            if let Some(absolute) = absolute {
              if imports.insert(absolute) {
                stack.push(asts.get(absolute).unwrap());
              }
            }
          }
          Item::Module {
            absolute,
            doc,
            groups,
            name,
            ..
          } => {
            if let Some(absolute) = absolute {
              Self::define(&mut definitions, *name, "module", false)?;
              self.modules.insert(Self::analyze(
                asts,
                doc.clone(),
                groups.as_slice(),
                loaded,
                Some(*name),
                paths,
                absolute,
              )?);
            }
          }
          Item::Recipe(recipe) => {
            if recipe.enabled() {
              Self::analyze_recipe(recipe)?;
              self.recipes.push(recipe);
            }
          }
          Item::Set(set) => {
            self.analyze_set(set)?;
            self.sets.insert(set.clone());
          }
          Item::Unexport { name } => {
            if !self.unexports.insert(name.lexeme().to_string()) {
              return Err(name.token.error(DuplicateUnexport {
                variable: name.lexeme(),
              }));
            }
          }
        }
      }

      self.warnings.extend(ast.warnings.iter().cloned());
    }

            optional,

            ..

            ..

            optional,
            relative,
            ..
          } => {
            let parent = current.path.parent().unwrap();

            let relative_path = relative
              .as_ref()
              .map(|relative| Self::expand_tilde(&relative.cooked))
              .transpose()?;

            let name_value = *name;
            let import = Self::find_module_file(parent, name_value, relative_path.as_deref())?;
